<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">
 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;2.02. Results of Operations and Financial Condition. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On August&#160;3, 2023, we issued the press release furnished as Exhibit 99.1. The press release describes the results of our operations for the quarter and fiscal year ended June&#160;30, 2023. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information furnished in this Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> under Item 2.02 and the attached exhibit shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such a filing. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;8.01. Other Events. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On August&#160;3, 2023, we announced that our board of directors declared a quarterly cash dividend of US $0.48 per share. The dividend will have a record date of August&#160;17, 2023, payable on September&#160;21, 2023. The dividend will be paid in U.S. currency to holders of ResMed&#8217;s common stock trading on the New York Stock Exchange. Holders of CHESS Depositary Instruments trading on the Australian Securities Exchange will receive an equivalent amount in Australian currency, based on the exchange rate on the record date, and reflecting the 10:1 ratio between CDIs and NYSE shares. The <span style="white-space:nowrap">ex-dividend</span> date will be August&#160;16, 2023, for common stockholders and for CDI holders. ResMed has received a waiver from the ASX&#8217;s settlement operating rules, which will allow ResMed to defer processing conversions between its common stock and CDI registers from August&#160;16, 2023, through August&#160;17, 2023, inclusive.</p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;9.01. Financial Statements and Exhibits. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Exhibits </p> <p style="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ResMed Inc. Announces Results for the Fourth Quarter of Fiscal Year 2023 </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#150;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><I>Year-over-year revenue grows 23%, operating profit up 8%, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT>
operating profit up 13%</I> </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#150;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Quarterly dividend increases 9% to $0.48 per share </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Note: A webcast of ResMed&#146;s conference call will be available at 4:30 p.m. ET today at&nbsp;<U>http://investor.resmed.com</U> </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">SAN DIEGO, August&nbsp;3, 2023 &#150; ResMed Inc. (NYSE: RMD, ASX: RMD) today announced results for its quarter ended June&nbsp;30, 2023. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Fourth Quarter 2023 Highlights </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>All comparisons are to
the prior year period </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Revenue increased by 23% to $1.1&nbsp;billion; up 23% on a constant currency basis</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

contracted 200 bps to 55.8% </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

per share of $6.44 </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;ResMed&#146;s fourth quarter and full-year 2023 results reflect strong double-digit growth as we continue to
produce and deliver cloud-connected flow generator device volume to meet the ongoing strong global demand from patients, accompanied by high growth of our market-leading patient interface and software solutions,&#148; said Mick Farrell, Chairman and
CEO of ResMed. &#147;The combined global supply of our cloud-connected platforms, AirSense10 and AirSense11, have enabled us to support all available customer demand for CPAP and APAP devices across the global market. The strong growth of our mask
and patient interfaces business was </P>

supported by new patient setups as well as ongoing resupply activity as we focus on increasing therapy adherence to improve patient outcomes and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">quality-of-life.</FONT></FONT> Our residential medicine <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">software-as-a-service</FONT></FONT></FONT> business continues to
achieve high-single-digit growth organically expanding to solid double-digit growth including the contribution from MEDIFOX DAN. As we turn to fiscal year 2024, our focus remains on delivering world-leading therapy and digital health solutions so
that even more people are able to sleep better, breathe better, and live higher-quality lives outside the hospital, preferably in their own home. We continue to significantly grow our impact each quarter, improving over 160&nbsp;million lives in the
last 12 months, well on our way to helping 250&nbsp;million lives in 2025.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Financial Results and Operating Metrics </B></P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Discussion of Fourth Quarter Results </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>All comparisons are to the prior year period unless otherwise noted </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Revenue grew by 23&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, driven by increased demand for our sleep and
respiratory care devices as well as reduced competitive supply. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Software-as-a-Service,</FONT></FONT></FONT> grew by 25&nbsp;percent, primarily due to the factors discussed above. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Software-as-a-Service,</FONT></FONT></FONT> grew by 14&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

revenue increased by 34&nbsp;percent, reflecting incremental revenue from our acquisition of MEDIFOX DAN and continued organic growth in our SaaS portfolio. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Gross margin decreased by 210 basis points <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">and&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;gross</FONT>
margin decreased by 200 basis points, mainly due to unfavorable product mix and higher component and manufacturing costs, partially offset by an increase in average selling prices. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

expenses increased to 21.5&nbsp;percent of revenue in the quarter, compared with 21.1&nbsp;percent in the same period of the prior year. These changes in SG&amp;A expenses were mainly due to increases in employee-related expenses and incremental
expense associated with our acquisition of MEDIFOX DAN. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">and&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;income</FONT> from operations increased by 13&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

STYLE="white-space:nowrap">$1.56.&nbsp;Non-GAAP&nbsp;net</FONT> income increased by 7% to $235.5&nbsp;million, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">and&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;diluted</FONT> earnings per share increased by 7% to $1.60, predominantly
attributable to strong sales, partially offset by gross margin contraction. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

$229.7&nbsp;million and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> net income of $235.5&nbsp;million. During the quarter we paid $64.7&nbsp;million in dividends. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

software for sleep labs and physicians. Somnoware is upstream of and complementary to ResMed&#146;s current post-testing AirView and Brightree offerings and will remain an open platform. The transaction&#146;s financial terms are not material to
ResMed&#146;s consolidated financial results and were not disclosed. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

showed treating OSA with PAP lowered <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">all-cause</FONT> mortality, adaptive-servo ventilation (ASV) improved quality of life in central sleep apnea (CSA), and PAP
adherence lowered ER visits <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">24-36%</FONT> at <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-year</FONT> for OSA patients with heart failure, among others. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Announced the promotion of Michael Rider to Global General Counsel and Secretary, effective July&nbsp;1, 2023 and
Dawn Haake to Chief Quality Officer, effective May&nbsp;1, 2023. Mr.&nbsp;Rider was previously ResMed&#146;s Senior Vice President, Deputy Global General Counsel and has been with ResMed for over 10 years. Ms.&nbsp;Haake was previously ResMed&#146;s
Vice President, Quality Assurance and Regulatory Affairs and has been with ResMed for 8 years. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Dividend program </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The ResMed board of directors today declared a quarterly cash dividend of $0.48 per share. The dividend will have a record date of August&nbsp;17, 2023,
payable on September&nbsp;21, 2023. The dividend will be paid in U.S. currency to holders of ResMed&#146;s common stock trading on the New York Stock Exchange. Holders of CHESS Depositary Interests (&#147;CDIs&#148;) trading on the Australian
Securities Exchange will receive an equivalent amount in Australian currency, based on the exchange rate on the record date, and reflecting the 10:1 ratio between CDIs and NYSE shares.
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">The&nbsp;ex-dividend&nbsp;date</FONT> will be August&nbsp;16, 2023, for common stockholders and for CDI holders. ResMed has received a waiver from the ASX&#146;s settlement operating rules, which will allow ResMed to
defer processing conversions between its common stock and CDI registers from August&nbsp;16, 2023, through August&nbsp;17, 2023, inclusive.</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Webcast
details </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">ResMed will discuss its fourth-quarter fiscal year 2023 results on its webcast at 1:30 p.m. U.S. Pacific Time today. The live webcast of
the call can be accessed on ResMed&#146;s Investor Relations website at <U>investor.resmed.com</U>. Please go to this section of the website and click on the icon for the &#147;Q4 2023 Earnings Webcast&#148; to register and listen to the live
webcast. A replay of the earnings webcast will be accessible on the website and available approximately two hours after the live webcast. In addition, a telephone replay of the conference call will be available approximately three hours after the
webcast by dialing <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">+1&nbsp;877-660-6853&nbsp;(U.S.)</FONT></FONT> or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">+1&nbsp;201-612-7415&nbsp;(outside</FONT></FONT>
U.S.) and entering the passcode 13739812. The telephone replay will be available until August&nbsp;17, 2023. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>About ResMed </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">At ResMed (NYSE: RMD, ASX: RMD) we pioneer innovative solutions that treat and keep people out of the hospital, empowering them to live healthier,
higher-quality lives. Our digital health technologies and cloud-connected medical devices transform care for people with sleep apnea, COPD, and other chronic diseases. Our
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">comprehensive&nbsp;out-of-hospital&nbsp;software</FONT></FONT> platforms support the professionals and caregivers who help people stay healthy in the home or care setting of their
choice. By enabling better care, we improve quality of life, reduce the impact of chronic disease, and lower costs for consumers and healthcare systems in more than 140 countries.&nbsp;To learn more, visit&nbsp;<U>ResMed.com</U>&nbsp;and follow
@ResMed. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Safe harbor statement </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Statements

<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom">$</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom" ALIGN="right">5.79</TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD></TR>
</TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(A)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">ResMed adjusts for the impact of the amortization of acquired intangibles, restructuring expenses,
acquisition-related expenses, gain on insurance recoveries, (gain) loss on equity investments, reserves for disputed tax positions, and associated tax effects from their evaluation of ongoing operations, and believes that investors benefit from
adjusting these items to facilitate a more meaningful evaluation of current operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">ResMed believes <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">that&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;diluted</FONT> earnings per share is an additional measure of performance that investors can use to compare operating results between reporting periods. ResMed
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">uses&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;information</FONT> internally in planning, forecasting, and evaluating the results of operations in the current period and in comparing it to past periods. ResMed believes this information
provides investors better insight when evaluating ResMed&#146;s performance from core operations and provides consistent financial reporting. The use <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> is intended to supplement,
and not to replace, the presentation of net income and other GAAP measures. Like <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">all&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures,&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;earnings</FONT></FONT> are subject to inherent
limitations because they do not include all the expenses that must be included under GAAP. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">&#150; More &#150; </P>

</DIV></Center>

translate the current period financial information using the foreign currency exchange rates that were in effect during the previous comparable period. However, constant currency measures should not be considered in isolation or as an alternative to
U.S. dollar measures that reflect current period exchange rates, or to other financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with U.S. GAAP. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
